    "# Recover a supernova in Kepler data"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "This tutorial demonstrates how to recover a known supernova signal from the Kepler prime mission data.\n",
    "\n",
    "The Kepler prime mission observed about [500 galaxies over several years](http://adsabs.harvard.edu/abs/2015AJ....150..188S), discovering about a dozen supernovae and other extragalactic transients.  K2 continues extragalactic science, having observed over 40,000 galaxies.  Extragalactic science with K2 falls into two categories: **transient searches** and **active galactic nuclei** timescales.  In this tutorial we focus on the former."
   ]
  },
